screenshot" data-expand-target="full-screenshot-7" data-expand-to="thumbnails" data-expand-fit-screen="true" data-expand-scroll="true"> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="details-section-divider"></div> </div> <div class="details-section description simple contains-text-link"> <div class="details-section-contents show-more-container" data-show-use-buffer="true"> <div class="heading"> Description </div> <div class="show-more-content text-body" itemprop="description"> <div>★ New York Times ‘Top 10 Must-Have App’, Winner: TechCrunch Crunchies, Mashable Awards and the Webbys. ★  <p>Evernote is an easy-to-use, free app that helps you remember everything across all of the devices you use. Stay organized, save your ideas and improve productivity. Evernote lets you take notes, capture photos, create to-do lists, record voice reminders--and makes these notes completely searchable, whether you are at home, at work, or on the go. <p>Key Features:<br>- Works with Evernote Business: Capture, browse, search, and share Business Notes and Business Notebooks from your smartphone or tablet.<br>- Sync all of your notes across the computers and devices you use<br>- Create and edit text notes, to-dos and task lists  <br>- Save, sync and share files  <br>- Search for text inside images<br>- Organize notes by notebooks and tags<br>- Email notes and save tweets to your Evernote account<br>- Connect Evernote to other apps and products you use<br>- Share notes with friends and colleagues via Facebook and Twitter<br>★ Premium feature: take notebooks offline to access them anytime <br>★ Premium feature: allow others to edit your notebooks<br>★ Premium feature: add a PIN lock to your Evernote app<p>Here are some ways to use Evernote for your personal and professional life:<br>- Research smarter: snap photos of whiteboards and books<br>- Take meeting and class notes, draft agendas and research notes<br>- Plan a trip: keep track of travel plans, plane tickets and passports<br>- Organize and save recipes; search by ingredients later<br>- Create a grocery list or task list and check things off as you go<br>- View web pages saved in Evernote on your desktop<br>- Capture ideas and inspiration on the go<br>- Access files and notes you create on your phone from your desktop<br>- Keep track of products and prices for comparison shopping purposes<br>- Keep finances in order: save receipts, bills and contracts<br>- Reduce paper clutter by taking snapshots of restaurant menus, business cards and labels<br>- Use Evernote as part of your GTD system to help you stay organized<br>- To get the most out of your Evernote experience, download it on all of the computers and phones that you use.<p>Evernote is available on any computer, phone and tablet device.<p>More information about permissions at:<br><a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=http://evernote.com/privacy/data_usage.php&amp;sa=D&amp;usg=AFQjCNFlUahHSnW-ynRsrqd6cr1kxrsccA" target="_blank">http://evernote.com/privacy/data_usage.php</a><p><br>Learn more: <a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=http://www.evernote.com/about/getting_started/&amp;sa=D&amp;usg=AFQjCNFFdb7DO02Xm4QNNC36yfzvwKK8og" target="_blank">http://www.evernote.com/about/getting_started/</a></div> <div class="show-more-end"></div> </div>  <div class="play-button show-more small"> Read more </div> <div class="play-button you use. Stay organized, save your ideas and improve productivity. Evernote lets you take notes, capture photos, create to-do lists, record voice reminders--and makes these notes completely searchable, whether you are at home, at work, or on the go. <p>Key Features:<br>- Works with Evernote Business: Capture, browse, search, and share Business Notes and Business Notebooks from your smartphone or tablet.<br> - Sync all of your notes across the computers and devices you use<br> - Create and edit text notes, to-dos and task lists  <br> - Save, sync and share files<br> - Search for text inside images<br> - Organize notes by notebooks and tags<br> - Email notes and save tweets to your Evernote account<br> - Connect Evernote to other apps and products you use<br> - Share notes with friends and colleagues via Facebook and Twitter<br> ★ Premium feature: take notebooks offline to access them anytime<br> ★ Premium feature: allow others to edit your notebooks<br> ★ Premium feature: add a PIN lock to your Evernote app<p>Here are some ways to use Evernote for your personal and professional life:<br> - Research smarter: snap photos of whiteboards and books<br> - Take meeting and class notes, draft agendas and research notes<br> - Plan a trip: keep track of travel plans, plane tickets and passports<br> - Organize and save recipes; search by ingredients later<br> - Create a grocery list or task list and check things off as you go<br> - View web pages saved in Evernote on your desktop<br> - Capture ideas and inspiration on the go<br> - Access files and notes you create on your phone from your desktop<br> - Keep track of products and prices for comparison shopping purposes<br> - Keep finances in order: save receipts, bills and contracts<br> - Reduce paper clutter by taking snapshots of restaurant menus, business cards and labels<br> - Use Evernote as part of your GTD system to help you stay organized<br> - To get the most out of your Evernote experience, download it on all of the computers and phones that you use. </span> </span>  </span> </div> <div class="description">  Color Note is a simple notepad app. It gives you a quick and simple notepad editing experience when you write notes, memo, email, message, shopping list and to do list. Color Note makes taking a note easier than any other notepad and memo apps.<p>*Notice*<br>If you cannot find widget, please read below FAQ. It is not a bug.<p>*Features*<br>-Organize notes by color<br>-Sticky Note Widget<br>-Checklist for To do list &amp; Shopping list<br>-Checklist to get things done (GTD)<br>-Organize your schedule in calendar<br>-Password Lock note : Protect your notes by passcode<br>-Secured backup notes to sd storage<br>-Supports online back up and sync. You can sync notes between phone and tablet.<br>-Reminder on status bar<br>-List/Grid View<br>-Search notes<br>-Notepad supports ColorDict Add-On<br>-Powerful Reminder : Time Alarm, All day, Repetition.(lunar calendar)<br>-Quick memo / notes<br>-Wiki link : [[Title]]<br>-Share notes via SMS, email, twitter<br>-Use color to categorize notes<p>* Online backup and sync cloud service *<br>-Notes will be encrypted before uploading using the AES standard, which is the same encryption standard used by banks to secure customer data.<br>-It does not send any of your notes to server without your signing up.<br>-Sign-in with Google, Sign-in with Facebook.<p>* About Permissions *<br>-Internet Access : For online backup &amp; sync<br>-Modify/delete SD card contents : For backup to sdcard<br>-Prevent phone from sleeping, control vibrator, automatically start at boot : For reminder<p>*FAQ*<br>Q : How do you put a sticky note widget on the home screen?<br>A : Goto home screen and long press empty space and choose widget, Color Note will be there for sticking on page. <p>Q : How come the widget and the alarm and remider functions don&#39;t work?<br>A : If the app is installed on the SD card, your widget, reminder and etc. will not work properly because Android doesn&#39;t support them! If you have already moved app to SD card, but you want those features, you have to move it back to device and reboot your phone.<p>Settings - Applications - Manage Applications - ColorNote - Move to Device<p>Q : Where is backed up notes data at sdcard?<br>A : /data/colornote on sdcard<p>Q: I forgot my master password, how can I change it?<br>A: Menu -&gt; Settings -&gt; Master Password -&gt; Menu Button-&gt; Clear Password. You will lose current locked notes when you clear password!<p>* Product Description *<br>Color Note notepad features two basic note taking formats, a lined-paper styled text option and a traditional checklist option. Add as many as you want to your master list, which appears on the app&#39;s home screen each time the program opens. This list may be viewed in traditional ascending order, in a grid format, or by the color of the note.<p>- Taking a Note -<br>Serving as a simple word processing program, the text option allows for as many characters as you&#39;re willing to type with your device&#39;s virtual or physical keyboard. Once saved, you can edit, share, set a reminder, check off or delete the note through your device&#39;s menu button. When checking off a text note, the app places a slash through the list&#39;s title, a mark that shows on the main menu.<p>- Making To do List or Shopping List -<br>In the checklist mode, you can add as many items as you&#39;d like and move their order around with the up and down buttons activated in the edit mode. After the list is finished and saved, you may check, and uncheck, each line on your list with a quick tap that generates a line slash. If all items have been checked, the list&#39;s title is slashed as well.<p>When you&#39;re finished using the notepad, an automatic save command preserves your individual note.<p>Keywords : Notebook, You&#39;ll know exactly what needs to get done, who&#39;s going to do it, and what&#39;s coming up next. And, everything you do is synced and saved instantly to Trello.com. Use the web site to stay organized while you&#39;re at your desk, and the app to stay up to date while you&#39;re out and about.<p><br>** How it works **<p>With Trello, you can create boards to organize anything you&#39;re working on. Use them solo, or invite friends, family, or colleagues to work together.<p>Write your ideas down on Trello cards and arrange them in lists on your boards. use just like paper, but with the flexibility and advantages of modern technology. With Papyrus, you can go beyond paper!<p>Papyrus allows you to take handwritten notes on your Android device using either an active pen (e.g. Samsung S Pen), passive stylus, or your finger. The vector graphics engine keeps your notes beautiful at any zoom level and on any device, while the simple and intuitive user interface allows you to take notes quickly and efficiently!<p>We&#39;d love to hear your feedback and feature requests at <a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=http://feedback.projectpapyrus.com&amp;sa=D&amp;usg=AFQjCNHRol5kBNzEeWQoCPkWvig4JiXMOg" target="_blank">http://feedback.projectpapyrus.com</a>.<p><b>Awards/Recognition</b><br> • Featured App in Google Play<br> • Category Honorable Mention for Productivity in the Samsung Galaxy Note S Pen App Challenge (<a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=http://goo.gl/M6gKK&amp;sa=D&amp;usg=AFQjCNFiFE3OxBVhqdMh9NOsxYGbLkfdUw" target="_blank">http://goo.gl/M6gKK</a>)<p><b>Premium Features</b>¹<br> • Tool Pack - Adds a &quot;true&quot; eraser tool (erase parts of strokes), shape tools, and a text tool<br> • Cloud Services - Backup/restore and export notes as PDFs to cloud storage providers such as Dropbox and Box<p><b>Key Features</b><br> • Take notes naturally with a pen on active-pen enabled devices<br> • Take notes with your finger or passive stylus (if you don’t have an active pen)<br> • Pen strokes are vector graphics<br> • Undo/redo strokes<br> • Select, move, and resize strokes<br> • Change the color and weight of selected strokes<br> • Cut, copy, and paste strokes between notes<br> • Multiple paper types and sizes<br> • Two finger scroll<br> • Two finger pinch-to-zoom<br> • Two finger double tap to zoom to 100%<br> • Organize notes within notebooks (long press, drag and drop)<br> • Sort notes and notebooks<br> • Image import, crop, and resize<br> • Export notes to PDF, PNG, or JPEG for printing, archiving, or sharing<br> • Share notes with friends and colleagues via email, Evernote, and other services<br> • Samsung Multi-Window support (available on Galaxy Note 2, Note 8.0, and Note 10.1)<br> • Shortcuts to create a new note or open a notebook<p><b>Active Pen Device Exclusive Features</b><br> • Pressure sensitive pen for more natural writing<br> • Use pen side button to select pen strokes without having to switch tools<br> • Use pen side button for quick flick gestures (undo/redo and tool/color popups)<br> • Choose primary and secondary side button options<br> • Use pen eraser to quickly and naturally erase writing<p><b>Active Pen Device support includes</b><br> • HTC Flyer, HTC Jetstream, HTC EVO View 4G (HTC Scribe Pen)<br> • Lenovo ThinkPad Tablet<br> • Samsung Galaxy Note, Galaxy Note 2, Galaxy Note 8.0, and Galaxy Note 10.1 (S </div> <div class="description">  Take notes even when you don&#39;t feel like typing!  Just speak your note, and it will be saved as text.  This notepad app was designed to quickly jot down your ideas, with minimal hassle.  And it makes it easy to keep those ideas organized.<p>Features:<p>* Hands-free speech recognition at the press of a single button.<p>* Searchable.  Notes are indexed for fast searching.<p>* Password protection option for notes.<p>* Share notes with SMS, email, Twitter, and any other app that accepts plain text.<p>* Quickly add notes.  If you have a slide out keyboard, just slide it out and start typing.<p>* Accepts plain text from other apps that share.<p>* Password locked notes are encrypted beyond the first 20 characters.  This allows you to be able to identify and search for the note, while at the same time have the rest of it encrypted with the AES encryption standard.  This is the same encryption standard used by the US government and banks.<p>* Star notes with star filtering.<p>* Color-code notes and filter your list by color.<p>* Organize notes by category.<p>* Deleted notes are moved to the trash so you have a chance to restore them.<p>Added Features:<p>* SD Card Backup and Restore.  Lets you make a backup of all your notes and stores them encrypted on your SD card.<br>* Continue button after creating your voice note, so you can add additional speech text if needed.<br>* Time to Breathe option - lets you choose how long to wait before stopping speech input.<br>* Full Screen and popup screen text editors.<br>* Quotation marks.  You can now say Quotation Mark and it will place one in your note.<br>* Carriage Return.  You can say Carriage Return to simulate pressing the Enter key.<br>* Category Sharing.  You can share/export an entire category of notes.<br>* Light and Dark Themes.<p>Popular uses:<p>* Text editor.  This is the classic note pad functionality.  ListNote works well as a scratchpad, memopad, or note book - much like the classic android apps colornote, ak notepad, and note everything, but with more speech-to-text functionality.<br>* Quick and easy note taking with speech to text.  Your voice is &quot;recorded&quot; as text.  Does not function as an actual voice recorder though.<br>* You can create a to do list, also refered to as a ToDo list, or 2do list.  Similar to list maker apps such as anydo (any.do) or mobislenotes, but with voice recognition as a more integral part.<br>* Task list.  Like other free notepad apps such as wunderlist, astrid, or gtd, but with speech recognition playing a more prominent role.<br>* Shopping list.  Great when you want to quickly write down something you&#39;ll need at the grocery store.<br>* Notebook organized with color tabs.  You can make a color note tab by long-pressing a note and selecting &quot;Change Tab Color&quot;.<br>* Simple notetaking.  Many people prefer a notepad app that doesn&#39;t require you to make an account and upload all your notes to a server like Evernote or Springpad.  There is no account necessary with ListNote.  All your notes are stored on your own device.<br>* Dictation software.  You can transcribe your thoughts quickly and easily.  You can then edit the result like you would with any text pad or scratch pad.  When you&#39;re editing the notes with the textpad, you can insert speech anywhere in the text, and even undo the last speech input if it didn&#39;t turn out right.<br>* Memo pad.  Works great as a memo app, much like others such as inkpad, mobisle, and catch, but with a different feature set.<br>* Secure notes.  You can create safe notes that are private.  These private notes are locked with password protection.  When you lock a note it&#39;s an easy way to encrypt text from prying eyes.<p>Requirements:<p>* Google voice search is required for speech to text functionality to work.  Most devices come with it pre-installed.  If you don&#39;t want to use the speech recognition functions, the app is still fully functional without it. <span class="paragraph-end"></span> <a class="card-click-target" <span class="price buy">   <span>$4.18</span>    </span> <span style="display:none" class="consume-label"> <a style="display:none" class="consume-link no-nav track-click" href="#" data-uitype="218" </span> <span style="display:none" class="consume-link no-nav watch-button track-click" data-video-docid="com.acadoid.lecturenotes" data-uitype="218"> Watch </span> <span class="price buy track-click" data-uitype="221"> Installed </span> </span> <span style="display:none" class="acquired-label"> <span class="acquired-icon"></span> </span> </span>  </span> </div> <div class="description">  LectureNotes is an Android app for note-taking by handwriting on the screen, in particular with a stylus.<p>It is designed while having a user at university (or at school) in mind, for instance a lecturer who is using it for preparing her/his lecture or even for actual teaching (by writing on the device and projecting the screen content for the audience) or a student who is using it for taking handwritten notes during a lecture. However, it has found many users outside university, for instance businesspersons who use it for business notes and sales presentations or artists who use it to create sketches and drawings.<p>Its major target devices are tablets with Android 3.0 or later (it is developed on a Lenovo ThinkPad Tablet with an N-trig stylus, a Samsung Galaxy Note 10.1 with an S-pen, and an Asus Nexus 7, a Samsung Nexus 10, and an Amazon Kindle Fire HD with an Adonit Jot Pro and a Wacom Bamboo stylus). The basic functionality should work on all devices with Android 3.0 or later, but some which are hardware-dependent such as pressure sensitivity might not.<p><b>NOTE:</b> There is a free trial version to test if the app is right for you. The free trial version is fully functional with the exception that the number of notebooks is constrained to two, with no more than eight pages per notebook.<p><b>User feedback:</b><br>We would love to hear from you, please send feedback and feature requests to us by email (devel [a] acadoid.com). If you encounter a problem with the app, please email us and we will do our very best to fix it quickly.<p><b>Major features:</b><br>* Requires only minimal permissions and no internet connection (we do respect your privacy!)<br>* Allows multiple pages to be simultaneously visible on the screen (i.e. continuous page view)<br>* Allows smooth writing, typing, scrolling, and zooming<p><b>Additional features:</b><br>* Allows free choice of notebook&#39;s page width and height (i.e. horizontal and vertical resolution of pages&#39; bitmaps)<br>* Allows free choice of notebook&#39;s cover color, paper color, paper pattern type (plain, ruled, checkered, image, or custom), paper pattern size, and paper pattern color<br>* Provides four standard pencil colors, three standard pencil widths, seven standard eraser sizes, and twelve custom pencils (for which color, width, softness, and pressure or velocity sensitivity can be freely chosen)<br>* Provides a text layer for entering text via keyboard<br>* Provides simple drawing tools such as line, empty and filled rectangle, empty and filled oval or circle, and text<br>* Allows cut, copy, and paste within notebook pages and across notebooks<br>* Allows multiple layers in notebook pages<br>* Allows image and image set import into notebook (including image import directly from camera)<br>* Allows single- and multi-page PDF import (requires PDFView to be installed)<br>* Allows notebook export as compressed PDF<br>* Allows notebook export to Evernote (requires Evernote app to be installed)<br>* Allows audio recording and replay (requires LectureRecordings to be installed)<br>* Allows video recording and replay (requires LectureVideos to be installed)<br>* Allows sharing of notebook pages<br>* Allows keyword attachment to notebook pages and automatic indexing<br>* Allows insertion, deletion, and rearrangement of notebook pages<br>* Allows sharing and import of notebooks<br>* Allows organization of notebooks in folders<br>* Allows backup and restore of notebooks board<p><b>Possible issue:</b> For certain functionality, the app requires other apps to be installed: Notebook import, notebooks board restore, and image set import require a file manager app to be installed; image import directly from camera requires a camera app to be installed; PDF import requires a file manager app and PDFView to be installed; export to Evernote requires the Evernote app to be installed; audio recording and replay require LectureRecordings to be installed; video recording and replay require LectureVideos to be installed. <span class="paragraph-end"></span> <a class="card-click-target" href="/store/apps/details?id=com.acadoid.lecturenotes"></a>  </div> </div>  <div class="reason-set"> <a Evernote is required in order to use the Evernote Widget app**<br>The Evernote Widget lets you go directly to core Evernote features right from your home screen.<p>3 widget options:<p>- List widget (Android 3.0+): Provides a scrollable list and display reminders. <br>- Large widget: Same as the small widget, plus snippets of recently viewed notes.<br>- Small widget: Create new text, snapshot and audio notes, and jump to the search screen.<p>How to install:<br>Once you install this app, tap and hold on the home screen, then select your preferred widget from the popup.<p>The story behind this widget:<br>We want every users to have the best Evernote experience possible. Unfortunately, if Evernote is installed on the SD card, then the widgets that comes with the app are unavailable. Thanks to this Evernote Widget application, anyone can take advantage of this time saving feature regardless of where Evernote is installed.<p>Learn more about the widget: <br><a Skitch.<p>Skitch lets you communicate your ideas in an instant. Annotate images and documents with arrows, stamps, shapes, text, and more. Use Skitch to mark up a PDF, snap your screen, annotate a photo, or create something new with a blank canvas. Then, share your thoughts and ideas with friends or co-workers. Getting everything done just right has never been easier.<p>Fast, friendly feedback<br>• Use shapes, text, stamps, highlighter and arrows to give quick feedback on any project<br>• Great for design mockups, PDF document editing, and decision making<br>• Easily share everything with your team<p>Perfect screenshots<br>• Snap your screen, a webpage or a map<br>• Add highlights and draw attention to what matters<p>Quick image editing<br>• Zoom and crop your images<br>• Pixelate portions of an image to obscure sensitive information<p>Simple sharing<br>• Share your work directly to the camera roll to use your it with any app that accepts images<br>• Share over email or connect to Evernote for even more sharing options<br>• Send annotated PDFs with a helpful summary page so recipients see your edits instantly<p>Get more by signing into Evernote:<br>• Sync: Access all of your images, documents and annotations on any computer or device<br>• Search: Find anything, even handwritten text, inside your Skitch Notes<br>• Share: Post and share your ideas with friends, coworkers and the world<p>Here are some ways to use Skitch:<br>• At work: Communicate design feedback by annotating a PDF and pointing out changes<br>• At home: Annotate a photo of your living room to show movers where to put furniture<br>• At a conference: Take a snapshot of people you meet, annotate it with their names<br>• For personal information: Take a photo of a bill, then pixelate personal details before sharing<br>• For directions: Draw a path on a map to help someone find your picnic spot<p>Skitch is part of the Evernote family of apps that are designed to help you remember everything, communicate effectively and get things done.<p>Skitch uses the contacts permissions in order to populate the email field when sending a PDF.
